Ok,  the F1 car has an insane budget. You have to bear in mind the relentless restrictions put upon the F1 over the years. In fact most of the budget is generated because of those restrictions and eecking out what you can. The banning of turbos cars, the banning of active suspension, the banning of launch control, the list goes on and on.. The road going cars only have to pass road safety specifications with no real limitations on performance as long as the local joey can drive it. The Mclaren 1988 MP4 had around 1200bhp...........Just imagine what we would have had 32 years later had there not been the restrictions that were in place in F1 on maybe half the budget.

That's the thing about F1 cars. They are designed to go INSANELY fast around corners, not in a straight line. Their straight-line speed is *aerodynamically* limited, unlike most road cars, which are either mechanically limited or electronically. They create so much downforce, they can only go so fast to overcome it.  Really fun race, but I'd like to see these things race the F1 car on the track.

So this video is very intriguing: 3 different power levels BUT with 3 consequently heavier vehicles. Since I know power to weight ratio is the common denominator for all three vehicles, and using "logic" and a little math I come up with the following power to weight ratios. Of course this is using the good old standard Horsepower ('MERICA) and the metric weight in KG. The F1's ratio is 1.15 HP per KG, the Lambo .773, and the GTR comes out to .707 HP per KG.    This means the F1 is putting 67% more HP per KG than the Lambo, and 61% more HP per KG than the GTR. On paper the F1 looks to be the winner before I even watch the video. But, this doesn't factor in traction with the F1 only being rear wheel drive and both the GTR and Lambo are AWD.  Should be fun, lets see what happens.......

It's a fake race, trust me. I'm Italian, and I love our cars, but there is no Lamborghini (or any road car) that goes faster than a Formula 1. Formula 1s go from 0 to 100 Km/h in 2 seconds, and from 0 to 200 in 4 or 5.The pilot of Formula  just didn't give full throttle. It is stupid just to compare a formula 1, which costs millions of euros, with a road car. Even more stupid is to believe that it goes slower.  If you listen well, you even hear that the pilot is not giving full throttle. If you don't know, the engines of the formula 1 can be set differently, so as to have more or less maximum speed, more or less short gears. And much more ...  Watch other videos of the acceleration of formula 1, you can visibly notice differences, in this video the driver spin the wheels at the start....you can see (3:32s.). Not everyone knows how to drive Formula 1 ... only experienced pilots. I also add that the engines of the formula 1, being very delicate, and after few races are replaced, and probably the one that was used in this video did not express its full power. This is nothing official. On the internet today you believe everything.  But what works is just the audience.  My personal opinion: today everything is evaluated for acceleration, but a Lotus Elise with 120 horsepower is better than cars that have four times that horse power, simply because the sportiness is in the curves, not on the straights. F1 cars are made to go the quickest around a track, both Lambo & GTR have no chance if they're put up against any F1 car in a track.

It's not very impressive when you think about how limited the F1 car actually is in comparison to the others.  Both the other cars are purpose built for straight line acceleration and top speed with no limits. The F1 car is built to maintain performance as efficiently as possible throughout an entire race circuit with restrictions. While it's entertaining to watch its not a realistic comparison.
